==================================================================================
Available commands:
t - Process turns  proceed to the next sequence in the game, eg the next computer 
player makes their turn 
hand - Show your hand and amount of gold you have
gold - Show your gold
citadel/list/city [player] - Show a player's citadel
actionCharacter - Show your character's action
actionDistrict - Show your district's abilities
useCharacterAbility - Use your character's ability
useDistrictAbility - Use one of your districts' ability (The cards in cards_to_implement.tsv are not implemented)
info [name] - Show info about a district in your hand or a character
build - Build a district
end - End your turn
all - Display info about all players, including number of cards in hand, gold and districts 
built in their city
help - Show this help menu
save [filename] - Save the game (Not implemented. This is hard af)
load [filename] - Load a game (Not implemented. This is hard af)
